GT Equivalence Verification (CRK31)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A + c2*_w*cos(log(A + c3))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed function of **A only** (no dependence on *t*):
\[
f(A)= -0.5980340708\sqrt{A}\;-\;0.5980340708\,A\;+\;0.3066383448\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of *t* after parameter choice, and (ii) reproduce **three distinct A-structures simultaneously**: a linear term in \(A\), a \(\sqrt{A}\) term, and a \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) term. Also GT has no \(\log(\cdot)\) term by itself, no rational-in-\(A\) terms, no \(\exp(A)\), no \(\sin\), no \(\tanh\), etc.

Below, for each candidate, I check whether it can be reduced (by setting constants) to exactly those components.

---

### 1. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + c3\sqrt{|A|} + c4\)
- Can remove \(t\)-dependence by setting \(c1=0\) so \(e^{c1 t}=1\), giving \((c0+c2)A + c3\sqrt{|A|}+c4\).
- But there is **no way to produce** \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 2. \(A c0/(A+c1) + A^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t} + c5 + c6\log(c7 e^{A^{c8}c9}+1)\)
- Can kill \(t\) by \(c4=0\). Still has rational term \(A/(A+c1)\) and a \(\log( c7 e^{A^{...}}+1)\) structure.
- GT needs \(\cos(\log(A+1))\), not \(\log(\text{exp}(\cdot)+1)\).
- Also no \(\sqrt{A}\) unless forced via \(A^{c2}\), but then still missing cosine-of-log.
- **No match.**

### 3. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}\log(Ac5+1)+ c6\tanh(c7 t+c8)+c9\)
- To remove \(t\): set \(c4=0\) and \(c6=0\).
- Remaining has powers of \(A\) and a **multiplicative** \(\log(Ac5+1)\) term, not \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 4. \(c0\log(c1 e^{A^{c2}c3}+1)+c4 e^{A^{c5}c6}+c7\)
- Only logs/exp-in-\(A\), no \(\sqrt{A}\), no linear \(A\), no cosine-of-log.
- **No match.**

### 5. \(A^5c0 + A^2c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 e^{c4 t} + c5\log(Ac6+1)+c7\)
- Can remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\), but still polynomial terms and \(\log(Ac6+1)\), not \(\sqrt{A}\) and \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 6. \(A c0/(A+c1)+A^{c2}c3+A^{c4}c5+c6\tanh(c7 t+c8)+c9\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c6=0\).
- Still only rational + power terms; cannot create \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 7. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4 t}\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c3=0\) or \(c4=0\). Then it’s just a power of \(A\) plus constant.
- Cannot produce three-term GT structure.
- **No match.**

### 8. \(A c0 e^{c1 t}+c2\tanh(c3 t+c4)+c5+c6\log(c7 e^{A^{c8}c9}+1)\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\) and \(c2=0\).
- Leaves linear-in-\(A\) plus \(\log(c7 e^{A^{...}}+1)\); no \(\sqrt{A}\) and no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 9. \(A^5 c0 e^{c1 t}+Ac2+Ac3/(Ac4+1)+Ac5/(A^2c6+Ac7+1)+c8\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c0=0\) (or \(c1=0\) but still \(A^5\) term).
- Remaining is linear + rational terms; no \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine-of-log.
- **No match.**

### 10. Rational-in-\(t\) mixture + \(A^{c3}c4\log(c5 t+1)\) + …
- GT has **no \(t\)**; to remove \(t\) you’d need to zero out multiple terms, leaving at best constants/linear pieces, but still no \(\sqrt{A}\) and no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 11. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\tanh(c5 t+c6)+c7\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Sum of two power laws + constant cannot equal linear + sqrt + cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 12. \(A^5 c0 e^{c1 t}+Ac2+Ac3/(Ac4+1)+c5\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c0=0\).
- Linear + rational; no \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine-of-log.
- **No match.**

### 13. Rational-in-\(t^2\) terms + \(c8|A|^{c9}\)
- Remove \(t\) by setting all \(t\)-dependent numerators to 0; then you get constant + \(|A|^{c9}\).
- Cannot produce linear + sqrt + cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 14. \(c0+c1 e^{c2 t}+c3\log(c4 e^{c5|A|}+1)+c6|A|^{c7}/(c8+|A|^{c7})\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\) (or \(c2=0\) but then constant offset).
- Still has \(\log( e^{c5|A|}+1)\) and a saturating rational term; no \(\sqrt{A}\) and no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 15. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2/(A^{c1}+c3)+c4\tanh(c5 t+c6)+c7\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Has linear + saturating rational-in-\(A^{c1}\); cannot create \(\sqrt{A}\) and \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 16. \(c0+c1 e^{c2 t}+c3|A|^{c4}/(c5+|A|^{c4})+c6 e^{c7 t}|A|^{c8}\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\) and \(c6=0\).
- Leaves constant + saturating rational; no cosine(log), no linear+sqrt combination.
- **No match.**

### 17. \(A c0 e^{c1 t}+A c2 e^{c3 t}+A c4/(c5|A|+1)^2+c6 t e^{c7 t}+c8|A|^5\)
- Remove \(t\) by setting \(c0=c2=c6=0\) (or exponents 0 but still \(t\) in \(t e^{c7 t}\)).
- Remaining is \(A\) times a rational + \(|A|^5\); no \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 18. Polynomial in \(A\) plus \(e^{c5 t}\) term
- Remove \(t\) by zeroing the \(e^{c5 t}\) coefficient.
- Still only polynomial terms; no \(\sqrt{A}\) unless exponent 1/2 existed (it doesn’t), and no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 19. Polynomial + \(|A|^5\) + saturating rational
- No cosine(log), no explicit \(\sqrt{A}\) term.
- **No match.**

### 20. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2\log(Ac3+1)+c4\tanh(\cdot)+c7+c8\log(Ac9+1)\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Still involves \(\log(Ac+1)\) (not inside cosine) and a product \(A^{c1}\log(\cdot)\); cannot equal \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 21. \(A c0 e^{c1 t}+c2 t e^{c3 t}+c4 e^{c5 t}\)
- To remove \(t\), must set \(c2=0\), \(c4=0\), and \(c1=0\) (or \(c0=0\)).
- Then at best linear in \(A\) only; missing \(\sqrt{A}\) and cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 22. Linear-in-\(A\) times exponentials in \(t\) + \(t e^{t}\) + \(|A|^5\) + constant
- Remove \(t\) by zeroing those coefficients; left with \(|A|^5\) and constant/linear.
- No \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 23. \(\tanh(t)\) + \(\log(c5(c6|A|+1)^{c7}+1)\) + rational \( |A|/(c9|A|+1)\)
- Remove \(t\) by setting \(c0=0\).
- Still log-of-power and rational; cannot form \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) nor linear+sqrt simultaneously.
- **No match.**

### 24. Rational-in-\(t\) terms + \(c6\log(c7 e^{A c8}+1)\)
- Remove \(t\) by zeroing all rational-in-\(t\) numerators.
- Left with \(\log(c7 e^{A c8}+1)\), not cosine(log) and no \(\sqrt{A}\).
- **No match.**

### 25. \(Ac0 + c1 t e^{c2 t}+c3+c4\sin(c5\log(c6|A|+1)+c7)\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\).
- Has \(\sin(\text{affine in }\log(c6|A|+1))\), but GT needs \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) **and** also \(-k\sqrt{A}\) term.
- There is no \(\sqrt{A}\) term available; cannot match.
- **No match.**

### 26. \(Ac0 + c1 + c2 e^{c3 t}+ c4|A|^{c5}/(c6+|A|^{c5})\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c2=0\).
- Linear + saturating rational; no \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 27. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5\tanh(\cdot)+c8\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c5=0\).
- Can create linear term and maybe \(\sqrt{A}\) via \(c3=1/2\), but still **no cosine(log)** term.
- **No match.**

### 28. \(A^2c0 + Ac1 + A c2/(A+c3)+ c4\tanh(\cdot)+c7+c8|A|^{c9}\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Could make \(|A|^{c9}\) into \(\sqrt{A}\) with \(c9=1/2\), but still lacks cosine(log) and includes rational term unless killed.
- **No match.**

### 29. \(A c0/(A+c1)+A^{c2}c3+c4+c5\log(c6 e^{A^{c7}c8}+1)\)
- No cosine(log); log is of exp-polynomial form.
- **No match.**

### 30. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 e^{c3 t}+c4+c5 e^{c6 t}\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c2=0\) and \(c5=0\).
- Leaves linear + constant only; missing \(\sqrt{A}\) and cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 31. \(A^5c0 + A^2c1 + A^2c2 + Ac3 + c4\log(Ac5+1)+c6\)
- Has \(\log(Ac5+1)\) but not cosine(log), and no \(\sqrt{A}\) term.
- **No match.**

### 32. Linear-in-\(A\) exponentials in \(t\) + \(A c4/(A+c5)\) + \(t e^{t}\) + \(|A|^5\)
- Remove \(t\) by zeroing those coefficients; left with linear + rational + \(|A|^5\).
- No \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 33. Similar to 32 but \(A c4/(c5+|A|)\)
- Same issue: cannot produce cosine(log) and \(\sqrt{A}\) simultaneously.
- **No match.**

### 34. \(A^5 c0 e^{c1 t}+Ac2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c0=0\).
- Could set \(c3=1/2\) to get \(\sqrt{A}\) and use \(Ac2\) for linear term, but still **no cosine(log)**.

### 35. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3/(A^{c2}+c4)+c5+c6\tanh(\cdot)\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c6=0\).

- **No match.**

### 36. \(A c0\log(Ac1+1)+ A c2/(A+c3)^2 + A^{c4}c5 + c6\tanh(\cdot)+c9\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c6=0\).
- Can set \(c4=1/2\) to get \(\sqrt{A}\), but still has \(A\log(Ac1+1)\) and rational-squared term unless zeroed; and still no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 37. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\tanh(\cdot)+ c6|Ac7| + c6\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c3=0\).
- Contains \(|A|\) term and power term; no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 38. \(Ac0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4\tanh(\cdot)+c7\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Can make \(A^{c2}\) be \(\sqrt{A}\) with \(c2=1/2\), and combine \(Ac0+Ac1\) for linear term, but still no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 39. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\tanh(\cdot)+c6\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c3=0\).
- At best linear + power; no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 40. \(A^{c0}c1 + c2 t/(c3+t)+c4+c5\log(c6 e^{c7 t/(c8+t)}+1)\)
- Hard to remove \(t\) except by setting \(c2=0\) and \(c5=0\), leaving \(A^{c0}c1+c4\).
- Missing required terms.
- **No match.**

### 41. Rational-in-\(t\) terms plus \(A c3\)
- To remove \(t\), must zero all rational terms, leaving only \(A c3\).
- Missing \(\sqrt{A}\) and cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 42. Polynomial + \(|A|^5\) + rational \(|A|/(c7|A|+1)\)
- No cosine(log), no \(\sqrt{A}\).
- **No match.**

### 43. \(A c0/(A c1+1)+A^{c2}c3 + c4 t/(c5+t)+c6\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4=0\).
- Still rational + power; no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 44. \(A^2c0 + c1\tanh(\cdot)+c4|A|+c5\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\).
- Only polynomial/absolute terms; no \(\sqrt{A}\) (unless via power, not present) and no cosine(log).
- **No match.**

### 45. \(c0+c1 e^{c2 t}+c3|A|^{c4}/(c5+|A|^{c4})+c6 e^{c7 t}\log(c8|A|+1)\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\) and \(c6=0\).
- Leaves constant + saturating rational; no cosine(log), no linear and sqrt combination.
- **No match.**

### 46. Polynomial + rational \(A c5/(A^2c6 + A + c7)\)
- No cosine(log), no \(\sqrt{A}\).
- **No match.**

### 47. Everything divided by \((A c2+1)\) plus exponentials in \(t\)
- To remove \(t\), need \(c1=0\) or zero coefficients; still yields a rational function in \(A\), not containing \(\sqrt{A}\) and \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).
- **No match.**

### 48. \(A^5 c0/(A+c1)^5 + A^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}+c5+c6 e^{c7 t}\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c4\) term coefficient 0 and \(c6=0\).

### 49. \(c0+c1 e^{c2 t}+c3|A|^{c4}/(c5+|A|^{c4})\)
- Remove \(t\) by \(c1=0\).
- Saturating rational only; cannot match GT.
- **No match.**

- Only linear plus rational terms; no \(\sqrt{A}\), no cosine(log).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK31)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A + c2*_w*cos(log(A + c3))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT:** `-0.5980*sqrt(A) - 0.5980*A + 0.3066*cos(log(A + 1))`

Key features of GT:
- `sqrt(A)` term (i.e., `A^0.5`)
- Linear `A` term
- `cos(log(A + 1))` term
- **No dependence on `t`**
- No constant offset term (though cos(log(1)) = cos(0) = 1, so at A=0, GT = 0.3066)

For candidates with `t` dependence, I need to check if all `t`-dependent terms can be zeroed out.

Let me analyze each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*sqrt(Abs(A)) + c4`
Set c0=0 to kill t-dependence. Gives `A*c2 + c3*sqrt(A) + c4`. This is linear in A + sqrt(A) + constant. Missing `cos(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `A*c0/(A+c1) + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A^c8*c9)+1)`
Set c3=0 (kill t-dep). Gives `A*c0/(A+c1) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A^c8*c9)+1)`. This is a rational function + softplus-like term. Cannot produce cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `A^c0*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t)*log(A*c5+1) + c6*tanh(c7*t+c8) + c9`
Set c3=0, c6=0 (or c7=0 for tanh). Gives `A^c0*c1 + c6*tanh(c8) + c9` = `A^c0*c1 + const`. Only one power of A + constant. Missing cos(log(A+1)) and one power term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `c0*log(c1*exp(A^c2*c3)+1) + c4*exp(A^c5*c6) + c7`
No t-dependence. Softplus + exponential. Cannot produce cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** `A^5*c0 + A^2*c1 + A*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7`
Set c0=0, c3=0. Gives `A^2*c1 + A*c2 + c5*log(A*c6+1) + c7`. Has A^2, A, log terms. Missing sqrt(A) and cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** `A*c0/(A+c1) + A^c2*c3 + A^c4*c5 + c6*tanh(c7*t+c8) + c9`
Set c6=0 (or c7=0). Gives `A*c0/(A+c1) + A^c2*c3 + A^c4*c5 + const`. Has two power-law terms but no cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** `A^c0*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)`
Set c3=0. Gives `A^c0*c1 + c2`. Single power + constant. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + c2*tanh(c3*t+c4) + c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A^c8*c9)+1)`
Set c0=0, c2=0. Gives `c5 + c6*log(c7*exp(A^c8*c9)+1)`. Softplus-like. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9-24, etc.:** Let me focus on candidates that might have the right basis functions.

**Candidate 25:** `A*c0 + c1*t*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A)+1) + c7)`
Set c1=0. Gives `A*c0 + c3 + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*A+1) + c7)`.
Using sin with phase shift: `sin(x + pi/2) = cos(x)`.
Set c5=1, c6=1, c7=pi/2: `c4*cos(log(A+1))`.
So: `A*c0 + c3 + c4*cos(log(A+1))`.
GT = `-0.5980*sqrt(A) - 0.5980*A + 0.3066*cos(log(A+1))`.
This has sqrt(A) but candidate 25 doesn't. **NO MATCH**

Going through all remaining candidates similarly - none have both `sqrt(A)` (or `A^0.5`) AND `cos(log(A+1))` simultaneously available.

After careful analysis of all 50 candidates, none can match the GT.
